tranſlated duche engliſ • ye loue comforte entende ſtudye noble arte chyrur gia ye whiche called handyworke surgery vtyle profytable al entende occupye noble ſciens ye herein openly expreſt ſhewyd ſhalbe practyſed vſyd many one therin ignoran̄t yt wyll medle ther whyche neuer laboured neuer ſa poynt ye begynnynge endynge therof wherefore often tymes ſenc dayly chaunceth ſmall townes borowghs vyllages lyefarre ony good cyte great towne ye dyuerie people hurt dyſeaſed lacke cōnynge men taken hande yt barber yōge maiſters whome ſciens neuer dyſcloſed thynkynge wordes olde lernydmen ſay wel poſſible man ſholde brynge well good ende yt thynge whiche neuer hath lytell ſene ¶ thus ye yonge ſtudyntys mayſters ieruaūtes barber ſurgyens entende noble arte cōnynge beholde ouerſe rede diligēce lytell boke iheronims bruynſwyke borne straeſborowgh lyne salerne hathe great labour cōpyled ſet gadered togyder behoof great profyt lytell volume thynkynge many noble auctours dyuers bokys good ſpede thā ye parttaker al honour therof yt myſfortune fall bytwene handy boūde euery man bere charge hynder loſſes whiche moche alone ¶ fyftly wyſe dede ye prayſed diſcrete lerned men yt ſpeke whiche ſay deſyreth lerne wyll nat man ſholde hym neglygently ſpylt peryſhed thus mayye come yone poncpoſe honeſty pleaſure whiche ellys myght tourne yourgrete ſhame dyſpleſure ¶ alſo ye maye conſydere two maye better amende fawte thā one workeman wel parceyue fawtys owne worke alone tyll hath longe wrought vpō ellys nere hande fynyſhte hit ſomtyme euyll ipoſtyble mendyd pryncypally many operacyons belongyng ſurgery therfore whan ye go two pacyent take hede ye make dyſcorde▪ lyke wyſe whan preſent alone pacyent blame • abſente dyffame hym nat ye haue ſaye withe eche let ſecrete within blode ye woūde cā ſtaūchyd wt drynes yt layd ye woūde afore ſayd ye ſhall haue therfor rule wher wt cowrs ye blode may holpen ſtoppyd yt many ſondry wayes ſomtyme fortuneth wyll holpen byndynge contrary ſyde ouer agaynſt yt woundyd place ſomtyme rubbynge ſomtyme lettynge blodr another place ſomtyme wt boxinge ſomtyme ymagynacyō ſhe woūdyd parſon doth ymagyne thynke bledid nomore ¶ ſecōd rule maner ye ſhall vſe vtter dryenge namyd localia howe ſholde layd vpon woūde vayne dyuers maners occupied rulyd ſomtyme noyſe cauſeth one ſterte fere blode rōneth congelyth dryenge layd ſō tyme ſhall bynde rubbe cōtrarye parte ryght hande dyd blede ye ſholde rubbe lyft arme well vp downe rubbynge bynd wt wollen ſelue ege clothe tentent blode may rōne ſocour place ſo fore boūde bycauſe place ſo bledyng may ſtaūche nat ſully hole ſtoppyd lym̄e place myght ware ſtyffe leſe felyng deed thus may ye ye lyft hande ryght frome ye ryght ſyde heed lyft fote ye ſame maner may done boxyng fleemynge alſo cloſynge woūdyd parſon ſettynge wyndow heed outwardis ſe maner redde ſay alway hym bledyth nomore ye dyde fleem hym let blode helth thus ye naturall ſtrēgth enforcid blode ſtaūched heed pullynge contrary eere wounde party eere woū de couerynge eere lede bounde ſtyffe aboute eere let bande come downwarde fyrſt byndynge ſo often tyll heed well bounde maner mayſters bonony byndeth matter thā ſhall lye wounded place make matter better auoyde afore wrytten ix lernynges belongynge woundes heed ¶ item woundes heed begynnynge tyll ſure frō impoſtumacyon ſhall mitigatyue ſofte wounde ſure impoſtumacyon ſo muſt medecyns drynes dryenge without pryckynge lyke heed powder ſhall made thus leruynge mayſter auicenna ¶ heed powder take • ryos ilirica orobi farina mā na que eſt thus minutū arſſtologie corticibus radicis papaueris mayſtet brunus dothe herto mirrā sarcocollā sā guinem draconis lancfrancus whelmus alſo myrtillos nuces cypreſſi ¶ woūdes heed whiche fortune cuttynge without brekige brayne pā ne ca xxviii wounde ſymple without loſyng ye ſubſtaunce ſhall ſowed bounde heled lyke another wounde yf ſo wounde loſe ſubſtaunce • ſhall cauſe fleſſhe growe agayne tentes powder ſa • ues plaſters hele lyke another wounde ſowynge onely profytable ſymple wonnde heede alſo many grete woūdes ye heed cauſed departynge woundes •… de gyder chargeth alteracyon ayre whiche dothe moche harme moundes ſmale wounde cuttyuge gothe ne ye ſhall ſowe clenſe aforeſayd yf greter cuttyng wo •… de vpper parte heed ſhal ſowede ſyde put therin oyle rofes takynge away payne wounde cometh ſynewy pannycle couereth ye brayne pāne oyle alſo loſeth loſe bonys therin hangynge▪ may ye better taken •… oyle roſes alſo taketh awaye ye ſharpne •… pannycle within clenſed ho▪ oyle roſes aforeſayd rectyfyeth woundes payne dryueth away euyll dyſpoſy cyon ¶ woūdes heed come cuttynge brekynge brayne panne thrughe perced ca xxix ſmall woūde many mayſters call runulam cured lyke afore ſay de wounde without brekynge brayne panne ſuche wounde cometh moche matter bycauſe courſe matter may come downe ye ſmall cuttynge wounde gretter ſyde heed vpper parte ye heed wounde ſyde heed cured lyke ye fyrſt ſymple woū ye muſt put weke tente ne • ther parte ſyde wounde bycauſe yf ony matter cleuynge within ye ſo • e therwith may clenſe yf ye wounde vpperparte heed ye ſhall ſowe ſhall cu galienus ſexto terapenti wrytteth ſymple brekynge comyng ye mydle ij table craney therto nedefull take dyuers ſheres called narowe rugines may lyke grete therfore bone ye pacyent vncouered ſo muſt ye fyrſt take mooſt brodeſt ſheres rugine take 〈◊〉 ſheres narower take ſhalleſt ſhall tymes myddes ij table yf payne deſy none ſo ſhall ye cure haſtely wt drynes tyll brought ende wounde may ſowed rupture cuttynge wtout leſynge ſo ſhall occupy aforeſayd ſheres muſt wounde bregmate vpper parte heed wounde fyde heed galienus deſyreth inſtrumēt ſowynge clenſynge tentys vpon ſayth hath ſene bone matter cometh ſoit good place clenſe ¶ aforeſayde galienus wrought another parſone ſame maner aferede touche brayne bycauſe hardnes ſlepynge bone therfore made none hole thynkynge brayne ſholde come dfall maner fracture brekynge bone generall howe ſhall ryghted heled ca lix woūdes yt happe neth ye ſofte mēbres haue ſayd ſkyn̄e fleſſhe vaynes ſynewes vnto ye bone ſhall wryte ye harder dele fracture brekynge ye bone sōtyme ye bo ne breketh ouertwharte yt fracture wt brekynge ſmal peces bone yt comenly called fracture ſomtyme ye bone beten hurte vneuen brokē wt ſplenters yt one pece many peces depteth yt called fruſtralis ye bone broken wt peces somtyme brokē ouertwhart wt peces rente length called apertura rente token ye fracture brekynge yf brede length knowen wel ynoughe ſplentes peces ye ſhall fele peces ye fracture wyl prycke ye fleſſhe pacyent feleth pryckynge ouer place fracture mooſt whā tow che hande ¶ fracture rynyng cometh length ye bone worſer knowen well bounden cometh often tymes grete payne meuynge hardneth fracture payne mar rynge fleſſhe yf haue moche moyſtnes euyll bycauſe be▪ holpē tyme ye fayntnes muſt fyrſt amended ¶ fracture wounde
